                         label=project_slug,\n                            topic_type=\"project\",\n                            project_slugs=[project_slug],\n                            session_id=session_id,\n                        )\n                        result_id = await store.create_result(\n                            intent_id=intent_id,\n                            urgency=result.get(\"urgency\", \"normal\"),\n                        )\n                        if _broadcaster:\n                            await _broadcaster.broadcast(SSEEvent(\n                                event_type=\"result_created\",\n                                target_session_id=session_id,\n                               \"summary\": result.get(\"summary\", \"\"),\n                                    \"data\": result.get(\"data\", {}),\n                                    \"urgency\": result.get(\"urgency\", \"normal\"),\n                                }\n                            ))\n                except Exception as e:\n                    logger.error(f\"Intent processing failed: {e}\", exc_info=True)\n\n        asyncio.create_task(stream_results())\n\n        # Return acknowledgment immediately\n        return {\n            \"utterance_id\": utterance_id,\n            \"session_id\": session_id,\n            \"intent_count\": len(intent_ids),\n            \"intent_ids\": intent_ids,\n            \"status\": \"dispatched\",\n            \"message\": f\"Dispatched {len(intent_ids)} intents for parallel processing\",\n        }\n\n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"Dispatch error: {e}\", exc_info=True)\n        return JSONResponse(\n            status_code=500,\n            content={\"error\": f\"Dispatch error: {str(e)}\"}\n        )\n\n\n@app.post(\"/escalate\")\nasync def escalate_endpoint(request: dict):\n    \"\"\"\n    Escalate an    intent_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),\n        session_id=session_id,\n        utterance=utterance,\n        intent_type=intent_type,\n        project_slug=project_slug,\n        topic_id=topic_id,\n Server-Sent Events endpoint for canvas connections.\n\n    Provides real-time updates for:\n    - Topic changes\n    - New results\n    - Intent status updates\n    - Workload summaries\n\n    Sends workload summary on connect for reconnection support.\n    \"\"\"\n    broadcaster = get_broadcaster()\n\n    # Get or create session (preserve provided session_id)\n    store = await get_store()\n    session = await store.get_session(session_id)\n    if not session:\n        session_id = await store.create_session(session_id)\n        logger.info(f\"Created new session: {session_id}\")\n\n    # Register or update surface\n    if not surface_id:\n        surface_id = await store.register_surface(session_id, \"canvas\")\n        logger.info(f\"Registered canvas surface: {surface_id}\")\n        surface_type=\"canvas\",\n    )\n\n    # Send workload summary on connect\n    summary = await store.get_workload_summary(session_id)\n\n    async def event_stream():\n        try:\n            # Send initial connection event with workload summary\n            yield broadcaster._format_sse(\"connected\", {\n                \"surface_id\": surface_id,\n                \"session_id\": session_id,\n            })\n\n            yield broadcaster._format_sse(\"workload_summary\", summary)\n\n            # Send initial topic cards\n            if _topic_manager:\n                cards = await _topic_manager.get_active_topic_cards(session_id)\n                yield broadcaster._format_sse(\"topic_cards\", {\n                    \"cards\": [card.to_dict() for card in cards]\n                })\n\n            # Stream events\n            async for event_data in broadcaster.event_generator(connection):\n                yield event_data\n\n        except asyncio.CancelledError:\n            logger.info(f\"SSE stream cancelled for surface {surface_id}\")\n            raise\n\n    return StreamingResponse(\n        event_stream(),\n        media_type=\"text/event-stream\",\n )\n\n\n@app.post(\"/heartbeat\")\nasync def heartbeat(request: dict):\n    \"\"\"\n    Heartbeat endpoint for canvas to update surface last_seen.\n\n    Called periodically by the canvas to prevent   \"\"\"\n    Process user feedback for self-modification or component iteration.\n\n    Returns a diff for approval or confirmation of application.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not _feedback_processor:\n {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_c426d07a02424dcaac6b84fd","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t# aide-de-camp: Application Plan\n2\t\n3\t## Overview\n4\t\n5\taide-de-camp is a universal personal interface that accepts stream-of-consciousness voice and text input, routes it to parallel agents across any domain, and renders results as a live canvas of HTML cards or as synthesized audio narration. It is built on top of existing personal infrastructure and improves itself through conversational feedback after initial bootstrap.\n6\t\n7\tCLI invocation: `adc`\n8\t\n9\t---\n10\t\n11\t## Problem Statement\n12\t\n13\tManaging multiple active projects requires constant context-switching between dedicated tabs, terminals, and chat sessions. The input channel (typing into a specific Claude Code tab) is also the routing layer, and that conflation adds cognitive overhead. The same problem extends beyond coding: research, lookups, personal context, reminders — anything that requires knowing which system to ask before you can ask it.\n14\t\n15\taide-de-camp eliminates that overhead by providing a single input surface that routes automatically, dispatches in parallel, and returns organized results without requiring the user to know where to ask.\n16\t\n17\t---\n18\t\n19\t## Core Architecture\n20\t\n21\t### The Hot Path\n22\t\n23\t```\n24\tUser utterance (voice or text)\n25\t  → STT transcription (Web Speech API or whisper-stt)\n26\t  → Intent Router (one LLM call, haiku-class, ~500ms)\n27\t      output: [{project_slug, intent_type, urgency, utterance_fragment}, ...]\n28\t  → N parallel Fetch+Synthesize workers (one per intent thread)\n29\t      Fetch: deterministic code, executes command matrix based on intent_type\n30\t      Synthesize: one LLM call per thread (sonnet-class, ~1-2s)\n31\t      output: {data, summary, urgency}\n32\t  → Results streamed via SSE to active canvas\n33\t  → Cards rendered client-side using component templates\n34\t```\n35\t\n36\tTarget: < 3 seconds from utterance to first partial result on canvas. No Claude Code session startup on this path.\n37\t\n38\t### The Async Path\n39\t\n40\t```\n41\tTask-profile intent (research, coding, long-running work)\n42\t  → NEEDLE task bead created (br create)\n43\t  → Existing Claude Code workers pick up bead normally\n44\t  → Bead watcher detects closure event\n45\t  → Result written to session store results table\n46\t  → SSE push to active canvas (or Telegram if no canvas)\n47\t```\n48\t\n49\t### The Self-Improvement Path\n50\t\n51\t```\n52\tFeedback signal (explicit instruction or implicit engagement pattern)\n53\t  → Self-modification agent (Claude Code via NEEDLE task bead)\n54\t      reads target artifact (prompt file, registry YAML, component template)\n55\t      generates update\n56\t      surfaces diff to user\n57\t  → User approves → artifact written → hot-reloaded on next invocation\n58\t```\n59\t\n60\t---\n61\t\n62\t## Components\n63\t\n64\t### 1. Intent Router\n65\t\n66\t**Runtime:** Direct API call (haiku-class via ZAI proxy)\n67\t\n68\tOne LLM call per utterance. Receives the full utterance text, the project registry, and a segmentation prompt. Returns a JSON array of intent threads, each tagged with:\n69\t\n70\t```json\n71\t[\n72\t  {\n73\t    \"project_slug\": \"options-pipeline\",\n74\t    \"intent_type\": \"status\",\n75\t    \"urgency\": \"normal\",\n76\t    \"utterance_fragment\": \"has the options pipeline caught up?\"\n77\t  },\n78\t  {\n79\t    \"project_slug\": \"ibkr-mcp\",\n80\t    \"intent_type\": \"status\",\n81\t    \"urgency\": \"normal\",\n82\t    \"utterance_fragment\": \"what's the state of the ibkr mcp\"\n83\t  }\n84\t]\n85\t```\n86\t\n87\tIntent types: `status`, `action`, `brainstorm`, `lookup`, `reminder`, `self-modification`, `monitoring-config`\n88\t\n89\tThe router reads its segmentation prompt and the project registry from disk on each call — no caching. Hot-reload is automatic.\n90\t\n91\tAmbiguous intents: if confidence is below threshold, router returns an `intent_type: \"clarification\"` thread. The voice model or canvas handles the clarification round-trip before dispatching.\n92\t\n93\t### 2. Project Registry\n94\t\n95\t**Format:** YAML file, read per-invocation by the router\n96\t\n97\tDefines projects the router knows about:\n98\t\n99\t```yaml\n100\tprojects:\n101\t  options-pipeline:\n102\t    aliases: [\"the pipeline\", \"options\"]\n103\t    description: \"Options data pipeline on apexalgo-iad\"\n104\t    cluster: apexalgo-iad\n105\t    namespace: options\n106\t    intent_support: [status, action, brainstorm]\n107\t    workflows:\n108\t      deploy:\n109\t        steps: [ci-status, image-tag, argocd-sync, pod-status]\n110\t\n111\t  ibkr-mcp:\n112\t    aliases: [\"ibkr\", \"the mcp\"]\n113\t    description: \"IBKR MCP server\"\n114\t    cluster: apexalgo-iad\n115\t    namespace: ibkr-mcp\n116\t    intent_support: [status, brainstorm, lookup]\n117\t```\n118\t\n119\tUpdated by the self-modification agent. Hot-reloaded on every router call.\n120\t\n121\t### 3. Fetch Strand\n122\t\n123\t**Runtime:** Deterministic code, no LLM\n124\t\n125\tExecutes a command matrix based on `intent_type` and the project's registry entry. No LLM decisions — the commands are determined by the intent type and project config.\n126\t\n127\tExample command matrix for `intent_type: status`:\n128\t\n129\t| Source | Command |\n130\t|--------|---------|\n131\t| Pod status | `kubectl get pods -n {namespace}` |\n132\t| ArgoCD sync | `curl argocd-ro-api/applications/{app}` |\n133\t| Git log | `git -C {repo_path} log -10 --oneline` |\n134\t| Bead list | `br list --project {slug} --status open` |\n135\t| CI status | `kubectl get workflows -n argo-workflows -l project={slug}` |\n136\t\n137\tResults are structured data passed to the Synthesize strand. Fetch runs each source concurrently; partial results (from sources that respond first) are passed to Synthesize incrementally to support streaming output.\n138\t\n139\tA `fetch_coverage` field tracks which sources succeeded and which failed. Failed sources are surfaced as caveats in the result.\n140\t\n141\t### 4. Synthesize Strand\n142\t\n143\t**Runtime:** Direct API call (sonnet-class via ZAI proxy)\n144\t\n145\tTakes `{intent_spec, fetched_context}` → produces `{data, summary}`.\n146\t\n147\t- `data`: structured JSON matching the component library's expected schema for this intent type\n148\t- `summary`: 1-3 sentence narration suitable for audio mode\n149\t\n150\tSingle-turn inference. Reads its system prompt from a file per invocation (hot-reload). The synthesize prompt is the highest-leverage artifact in the system — it defines result format, detail level, and what fields to include.\n151\t\n152\tRuns once per intent thread in parallel across all active threads.\n153\t\n154\t### 5. Escalate Strand\n155\t\n156\t**Runtime:** Direct API call + `br create`\n157\t\n158\tFor task-profile intents that need durable async handling:\n159\t1. One LLM call to formulate a bead body from the intent + context\n160\t2. `br create` to create the bead in the appropriate project\n161\t3. Returns a pending-card spec with the bead reference\n162\t\n163\tThe bead watcher subsequently bridges bead closure to result delivery.\n164\t\n165\t### 6. Voice Model\n166\t\n167\t**Runtime:** Realtime API (OpenAI or Claude Realtime, persistent session)\n168\t\n169\tThe conversational layer. Receives transcribed utterances (or audio directly), calls `dispatch_intent()` tool to trigger routing, and narrates results at appropriate moments.\n170\t\n171\tTool calls are triggers, not queries. `dispatch_intent()` returns an acknowledgment immediately; results arrive out-of-band and are surfaced by the voice model at natural conversational pauses.\n172\t\n173\tThe voice model's system prompt controls narration style, batching behavior, urgency handling, and multi-turn topic tracking. Read per session-turn from a file (hot-reload).\n174\t\n175\tIn audio mode there is no canvas. The voice model reads `result.summary` directly. When a user transitions from audio to canvas, pending results are rendered using the component library and appear on canvas — session continuity means the canvas catches up.\n176\t\n177\t### 7. UI-Regen Agent\n178\t\n179\t**Runtime:** Claude Code via NEEDLE (task bead)\n180\t\n181\tSteward of the component library. Given a result's data shape:\n182\t1. Finds the best-fit existing component (semantic match against component descriptions)\n183\t2. If no good fit, generates a new component from scratch and stores it\n184\t3. Applies the component template to result data accounting for layout bucket\n185\t4. On feedback, iterates the component (updates library, triggers canvas re-render)\n186\t\n187\tMulti-step: reads library, generates or selects, writes back. Claude Code's file access and tool use make this the right runtime.\n188\t\n189\tCreated as a task bead; not on the hot path. Canvas updates in place when a component is versioned (SSE push: `component_updated: {component_id, version}`).\n190\t\n191\t### 8. Self-Modification Agent\n192\t\n193\t**Runtime:** Claude Code via NEEDLE (task bead)\n194\t\n195\tReads and writes the artifacts that encode system behavior:\n196\t- Router prompt (`prompts/router.md`)\n197\t- Project registry (`config/registry.yaml`)\n198\t- Strand prompts (`prompts/fetch.md`, `prompts/synthesize.md`, etc.)\n199\t- Urgency classifier prompt (`prompts/urgency.md`)\n200\t- Voice model prompt (`prompts/voice.md`)\n201\t- Monitoring config (`config/monitoring.yaml`)\n202\t- Exception routing rules (`config/exceptions.yaml`)\n203\t\n204\tWorkflow for every modification:\n205\t1. Read current artifact\n206\t2. Understand intent of change\n207\t3. Generate updated artifact\n208\t4. Surface diff to user (in canvas or narrated in audio mode)\n209\t5. On approval: write artifact, hot-reload takes effect on next invocation\n210\t6. aide-de-camp: Application Plan\n\n## Overview\n\naide-de-camp is a universal personal interface that accepts stream-of-consciousness voice and text input, routes it to parallel agents across any domain, and renders results as a live canvas of HTML cards or as synthesized audio narration. It is built on top of existing personal infrastructure and improves itself through conversational feedback after initial bootstrap.\n\nCLI invocation: `adc`\n\n---\n\n## Problem Statement\n\nManaging multiple active projects requires constant context-switching between dedicated tabs, terminals, and chat sessions. The input channel (typing into a specific Claude Code tab) is also the routing layer, and that conflation adds cognitive overhead. The same problem extends beyond coding: research, lookups, personal context, reminders — anything that requires knowing which system to ask before you can ask it.\n\naide-de-camp eliminates that overhead by providing a single input surface that routes automatically, dispatches in parallel, and returns organized results without requiring the user to know where to ask.\n\n---\n\n## Core Architecture\n\n### The Hot Path\n\n```\nUser utterance (voice or text)\n  → STT transcription (Web Speech API or whisper-stt)\n  → Intent Router (one LLM call, haiku-class, ~500ms)\n      output: [{project_slug, intent_type, urgency, utterance_fragment}, ...]\n  → N parallel Fetch+Synthesize workers (one per intent thread)\n      Fetch: deterministic code, executes command matrix based on intent_type\n      Synthesize: one LLM call per thread (sonnet-class, ~1-2s)\n      output: {data, summary, urgency}\n  → Results streamed via SSE to active canvas\n  → Cards rendered client-side using component templates\n```\n\nTarget: < 3 seconds from utterance to first partial result on canvas. No Claude Code session startup on this path.\n\n### The Async Path\n\n```\nTask-profile intent (research, coding, long-running work)\n  → NEEDLE task bead created (br create)\n  → Existing Claude Code workers pick up bead normally\n  → Bead watcher detects closure event\n  → Result written to session store results table\n  → SSE push to active canvas (or Telegram if no canvas)\n```\n\n### The Self-Improvement Path\n\n```\nFeedback signal (explicit instruction or implicit engagement pattern)\n  → Self-modification agent (Claude Code via NEEDLE task bead)\n      reads target artifact (prompt file, registry YAML, component template)\n      generates update\n      surfaces diff to user\n  → User approves → artifact written → hot-reloaded on next invocation\n```\n\n---\n\n## Components\n\n### 1. Intent Router\n\n**Runtime:** Direct API call (haiku-class via ZAI proxy)\n\nOne LLM call per utterance. Receives the full utterance text, the project registry, and a segmentation prompt. Returns a JSON array of intent threads, each tagged with:\n\n```json\n[\n  {\n    \"project_slug\": \"options-pipeline\",\n    \"intent_type\": \"status\",\n    \"urgency\": \"normal\",\n    \"utterance_fragment\": \"has the options pipeline caught up?\"\n  },\n  {\n    \"project_slug\": \"ibkr-mcp\",\n    \"intent_type\": \"status\",\n    \"urgency\": \"normal\",\n    \"utterance_fragment\": \"what's the state of the ibkr mcp\"\n  }\n]\n```\n\nIntent types: `status`, `action`, `brainstorm`, `lookup`, `reminder`, `self-modification`, `monitoring-config`\n\nThe router reads its segmentation prompt and the project registry from disk on each call — no caching. Hot-reload is automatic.\n\nAmbiguous intents: if confidence is below threshold, router returns an `intent_type: \"clarification\"` thread. The voice model or canvas handles the clarification round-trip before dispatching.\n\n### 2. Project Registry\n\n**Format:** YAML file, read per-invocation by the router\n\nDefines projects the router knows about:\n\n```yaml\nprojects:\n  options-pipeline:\n    aliases: [\"the pipeline\", \"options\"]\n    description: \"Options data pipeline on apexalgo-iad\"\n    cluster: apexalgo-iad\n    namespace: options\n    intent_support: [status, action, brainstorm]\n    workflows:\n      deploy:\n        steps: [ci-status, image-tag, argocd-sync, pod-status]\n\n  ibkr-mcp:\n    aliases: [\"ibkr\", \"the mcp\"]\n    description: \"IBKR MCP server\"\n    cluster: apexalgo-iad\n    namespace: ibkr-mcp\n    intent_support: [status, brainstorm, lookup]\n```\n\nUpdated by the self-modification agent. Hot-reloaded on every router call.\n\n### 3. Fetch Strand\n\n**Runtime:** Deterministic code, no LLM\n\nExecutes a command matrix based on `intent_type` and the project's registry entry. No LLM decisions — the commands are determined by the intent type and project config.\n\nExample command matrix for `intent_type: status`:\n\n| Source | Command |\n|--------|---------|\n| Pod status | `kubectl get pods -n {namespace}` |\n| ArgoCD sync | `curl argocd-ro-api/applications/{app}` |\n| Git log | `git -C {repo_path} log -10 --oneline` |\n| Bead list | `br list --project {slug} --status open` |\n| CI status | `kubectl get workflows -n argo-workflows -l project={slug}` |\n\nResults are structured data passed to the Synthesize strand. Fetch runs each source concurrently; partial results (from sources that respond first) are passed to Synthesize incrementally to support streaming output.\n\nA `fetch_coverage` field tracks which sources succeeded and which failed. Failed sources are surfaced as caveats in the result.\n\n### 4. Synthesize Strand\n\n**Runtime:** Direct API call (sonnet-class via ZAI proxy)\n\nTakes `{intent_spec, fetched_context}` → produces `{data, summary}`.\n\n- `data`: structured JSON matching the component library's expected schema for this intent type\n- `summary`: 1-3 sentence narration suitable for audio mode\n\nSingle-turn inference. Reads its system prompt from a file per invocation (hot-reload). The synthesize prompt is the highest-leverage artifact in the system — it defines result format, detail level, and what fields to include.\n\nRuns once per intent thread in parallel across all active threads.\n\n### 5. Escalate Strand\n\n**Runtime:** Direct API call + `br create`\n\nFor task-profile intents that need durable async handling:\n1. One LLM call to formulate a bead body from the intent + context\n2. `br create` to create the bead in the appropriate project\n3. Returns a pending-card spec with the bead reference\n\nThe bead watcher subsequently bridges bead closure to result delivery.\n\n### 6. Voice Model\n\n**Runtime:** Realtime API (OpenAI or Claude Realtime, persistent session)\n\nThe conversational layer. Receives transcribed utterances (or audio directly), calls `dispatch_intent()` tool to trigger routing, and narrates results at appropriate moments.\n\nTool calls are triggers, not queries. `dispatch_intent()` returns an acknowledgment immediately; results arrive out-of-band and are surfaced by the voice model at natural conversational pauses.\n\nThe voice model's system prompt controls narration style, batching behavior, urgency handling, and multi-turn topic tracking. Read per session-turn from a file (hot-reload).\n\nIn audio mode there is no canvas. The voice model reads `result.summary` directly. When a user transitions from audio to canvas, pending results are rendered using the component library and appear on canvas — session continuity means the canvas catches up.\n\n### 7. UI-Regen Agent\n\n**Runtime:** Claude Code via NEEDLE (task bead)\n\nSteward of the component library. Given a result's data shape:\n1. Finds the best-fit existing component (semantic match against component descriptions)\n2. If no good fit, generates a new component from scratch and stores it\n3. Applies the component template to result data accounting for layout bucket\n4. On feedback, iterates the component (updates library, triggers canvas re-render)\n\nMulti-step: reads library, generates or selects, writes back. Claude Code's file access and tool use make this the right runtime.\n\nCreated as a task bead; not on the hot path. Canvas updates in place when a component is versioned (SSE push: `component_updated: {component_id, version}`).\n\n### 8. Self-Modification Agent\n\n**Runtime:** Claude Code via NEEDLE (task bead)\n\nReads and writes the artifacts that encode system behavior:\n- Router prompt (`prompts/router.md`)\n- Project registry (`config/registry.yaml`)\n- Strand prompts (`prompts/fetch.md`, `prompts/synthesize.md`, etc.)\n- Urgency classifier prompt (`prompts/urgency.md`)\n- Voice model prompt (`prompts/voice.md`)\n- Monitoring config (`config/monitoring.yaml`)\n- Exception routing rules (`config/exceptions.yaml`)\n\nWorkflow for every modification:\n1. Read current artifact\n2. Understand intent of change\n3. Generate updated artifact\n4. Surface diff to user (in canvas or narrated in audio mode)\n5. On approval: write artifact, hot-reload takes effect on next invocation\n6. On rejection: discard\n\nSafety model:\n- Diffs before every application — no silent changes\n- All artifacts versioned; any update can be rolled back with one instruction\n- Confidence threshold: unambiguous changes (adding an alias) can auto-apply with notification; structural changes always require explicit approval\n\n### 9. Background Analysis Bead\n\n**Runtime:** Claude Code via NEEDLE (task bead, low priority)\n\nRuns on a schedule. Reads intent history and engagement signals from the session store, identifies patterns, proposes artifact updates.\n\nExamples:\n- \"User consistently drills into status results for more detail → propose adding causality fields to synthesize prompt\"\n- \"User ignores pipeline monitoring pushes for 5 days → propose lowering urgency tier\"\n- \"After deploy status, user always asks about pod logs within 2 minutes → propose speculative pre-fetch\"\n\nProposals are surfaced as cards on canvas for user review. Auto-apply only above a high confidence threshold.\n\n### 10. Bead Watcher\n\n**Runtime:** Daemon process, no LLM\n\nWatches for bead close events from NEEDLE workers. On close:\n1. Reads `session_id` from closed bead metadata\n2. Looks up active surface in session store\n3. Writes result to `results` table\n4. Fires SSE push to canvas or Telegram push if no canvas active\n\nPure I/O. Runs as a long-running process (Deployment, not a K8s Job per infrastructure conventions).\n\n---\n\n## Data Model\n\n### Session Store (SQLite)\n\n```sql\nsessions (\n  id          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  created_at  INTEGER,\n  last_active INTEGER,\n  primary_surface_id TEXT\n)\n\nsurfaces (\n  id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  session_id      TEXT,\n  type            TEXT,  -- 'canvas' | 'telegram' | 'audio'\n  state           TEXT,  -- 'active' | 'idle' | 'disconnected'\n  always_available INTEGER DEFAULT 0,  -- 1 for Telegram\n  last_seen       INTEGER\n)\n\nutterances (\n  id          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  session_id  TEXT,\n  raw_text    TEXT,\n  created_at  INTEGER\n)\n\nintents (\n  id           TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  utterance_id TEXT,\n  session_id   TEXT,\n  topic_id     TEXT,\n  project_slug TEXT,\n  intent_type  TEXT,\n  status       TEXT,  -- 'pending' | 'dispatched' | 'resolved' | 'cancelled'\n  bead_ref     TEXT,  -- set for task-profile intents\n  created_at   INTEGER,\n  resolved_at  INTEGER\n)\n\nresults (\n  id          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  intent_id   TEXT,\n  topic_id    TEXT,\n  session_id  TEXT,\n  summary     TEXT,\n  data        TEXT,  -- JSON\n  urgency     TEXT,  -- 'critical' | 'high' | 'normal' | 'low'\n  created_at  INTEGER,\n  surfaced_at INTEGER,\n  acked_at    INTEGER\n)\n\ntopics (\n  id           TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n  label        TEXT,","numLines":300,"startLine":1,"totalLines":659}}}

(deterministic, per intent type)\n374\t│   ├── synthesize/          ← synthesize strand (direct API call)\n375\t│   ├── escalate/            ← escalate strand (bead creation)\n376\t│   ├── watcher/             ← bead watcher daemon\n377\t│   ├── session/             ← session store (SQLite)\n378\t│   ├── canvas/              ← web frontend (SSE consumer, card renderer)\n379\t│   └── cli/                 ← adc CLI\n380\t├── data/\n381\t│   ├── session.db           ← session store\n382\t│   └── components.db        ← component library\n383\t└── docs/\n384\t    ├── research/            ← Deployment Model\n394\t\n395\taide-de-camp is a **live web application**, not a static site. The FastAPI server is the intelligence layer — it handles SSE connections, maintains session state, runs the router and synthesize strands, and serves the frontend HTML. There is no CDN path (no CF Pages).\n396\t\n397\t### Why not static\n398\t\n399\t- SSE connections are long-lived; CDNs cannot proxy them\n400\t- WebSocket for the Realtime API voice session requires a persistent backend\n401\t- The session store (SQLite) and artifact store (prompts, registry) require a writable filesystem\n402\t- Hot-reload depends on the running server reading updated files from disk on each invocation\n403\t\n404\t### Phased hosting\n405\t\n406\t**Phase 0 (Hetzner server directly)**\n407\t\n408\tRun FastAPI as a process on the Hetzner server itself, not in k8s. Simplest possible path:\n409\t- NEEDLE workers and the aide-de-camp server share the same filesystem\n410\t- Self-modification agent writes directly to `prompts/` and `config/` — hot-reload works without any coordination\n411\t- Expose via Tailscale (the server is already on the mesh); no ingress config needed\n412\t- SQLite DBs are local files; no PVC required\n413\t\n414\tNo container, no CI, no ArgoCD. Just `uvicorn src.main:app` managed by a long-running tmux session or systemd unit.\n415\t\n416\t**Phase 1+ (containerized, ardenone-cluster)**\n417\t\n418\tOnce session persistence and multi-surface routing are needed, containerize and move to k8s:\n419\t\n420\t```\n421\tDocker image: ronaldraygun/aide-de-camp\n422\tDeployment: ardenone-cluster, namespace: aide-de-camp\n423\tPVC: /data/ (SATA, ReadWriteOnce)\n424\t  /data/session.db        ← session store\n425\t  /data/components.db     ← component library\n426\t  /data/prompts/          ← hot-reloadable prompt files\n427\t  /data/config/           ← registry.yaml, monitoring.yaml, exceptions.yaml\n428\t```\n429\t\n430\tThe artifact store (prompts, registry) moves from the repo's working directory to the PVC. The self-modification agent updates artifacts via the aide-de-camp API (`PATCH /artifacts/{name}`), which writes to the PVC path the server reads from.\n431\t\n432\t### Traefik configuration for SSE and WebSocket\n433\t\n434\tTraefik's default response buffering breaks SSE. The IngressRoute needs:\n435\t\n436\t```yaml\n437\t# IngressRoute annotations\n438\ttraefik.ingress.kubernetes.io/router.middlewares: aide-de-camp-strip-prefix@kubernetescrd\n439\t\n440\t# Middleware: disable buffering, extend timeouts\n441\tapiVersion: traefik.io/v1alpha1\n442\tkind: Middleware\n443\tmetadata:\n444\t  name: aide-de-camp-streaming\n445\tspec:\n446\t  buffering:\n447\t    maxResponseBodyBytes: 0   # disable buffering\n448\t  headers:\n449\t    customResponseHeaders:\n450\t      X-Accel-Buffering: \"no\"\n451\t```\n452\t\n453\tServersTransport timeout:\n454\t\n455\t```yaml\n456\tapiVersion: traefik.io/v1alpha1\n457\tkind: ServersTransport\n458\tmetadata:\n459\t  name: aide-de-camp-longlived\n460\tspec:\n461\t  forwardingTimeouts:\n462\t    responseHeaderTimeout: 0    # no timeout on SSE streams\n463\t    dialTimeout: 5s\n464\t```\n465\t\n466\tDUCK-E's existing WebSocket IngressRoute config is the reference implementation for this cluster.\n467\t\n468\t### SQLite concurrency\n469\t\n470\tMultiple writers (bead watcher, background analysis bead, session handler) require WAL mode to avoid lock contention:\n471\t\n472\t```python\n473\t# On DB open\n474\tconn.execute(\"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL\")\n475\tconn.execute(\"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL\")\n476\t```\n477\t\n478\tWAL mode allows concurrent reads during writes and serializes multiple writers without blocking. For a personal single-user app, this is sufficient through Phase 3. A server database (Postgres) is not needed.\n479\t\n480\t### adc CLI connectivity\n481\t\n482\tThe `adc` CLI is a thin HTTP client. It talks to the running server over Tailscale:\n483\t\n484\t```bash\n485\t# ~/.config/adc/config\n486\tserver_url = \"http://aide-de-camp.ardenone.com\"   # or localhost in Phase 0\n487\t```\n488\t\n489\tNo local inference. The CLI sends requests to the FastAPI backend and streams the SSE response to the terminal. On the Hetzner server in Phase 0, `server_url = \"http://localhost:8000\"`.\n490\t\n491\t### CI/CD (Phase 1+)\n492\t\n493\tNew Argo WorkflowTemplate `aide-de-camp-build` on iad-ci:\n494\t- Docker build → `ronaldraygun/aide-de-camp`\n495\t- Update image tag in `jedarden/declarative-config` (k8s/ardenone-cluster/aide-de-camp/)\n496\t- ArgoCD syncs automatically\n497\t\n498\tSame pattern as every other containerized service in the stack.\n499\t\n500\t---\n501\t\n502\t## Technology Stack\n503\t\n504\t| Layer | Choice | Reason |\n505\t|-------|--------|--------|\n506\t| Backend | FastAPI (Python) | Reuse DUCK-E scaffolding; SSE + WebSocket support; async-native |\n507\t| STT | Web Speech API → whisper-stt fallback | Zero-latency browser-native; whisper-stt already deployed |\n508\t| Voice session | OpenAI Realtime API (via DUCK-E session handler) | DUCK-E scaffolding already built on this |\n509\t| LLM calls | ZAI proxy (`llm-proxy.ardenone.com`) | Pay-per-token, no subscription pressure on hot path |\n510\t| Task workers | NEEDLE + Claude Code | Existing infrastructure, unchanged |\n511\t| Session store | SQLite (WAL mode) | Lightweight, local, additive-only schema; single-user app |\n512\t| Artifact store | PVC-mounted filesystem (Phase 1+) / local filesystem (Phase 0) | Writable at runtime; hot-reload reads per-invocation |\n513\t| Frontend | Vanilla JS + Web Components | No build pipeline; SSE consumer + client-side card renderer |\n514\t| Phase 0 hosting | Hetzner server, local process | Simplest path; shared filesystem with NEEDLE workers |\n515\t| Phase 1+ hosting | ardenone-cluster, k8s Deployment | Behind existing Traefik + Tailscale ingress |\n516\t\n517\t---\n518\t\n519\t## Implementation Phases\n520\t\n521\t### Phase 0 — Minimal Viable Surface (~2 days)\n522\t\n523\tValidates the core question: does routing + parallel dispatch reduce friction?\n524\t\n525\t- Single HTML page: textarea + mic button (Web Speech API)\n526\t- `POST /dispatch` endpoint: router → N parallel synthesize calls → SSE stream\n527\t- Results appear as basic cards as agents resolve\n528\t- No persistence, no auth, no component library, no ambient push\n529\t\n530\tDeliverable: the core query loop working end-to-end.\n531\t\n532\t### Phase 1 — Session and Topics (~1 week)\n533\t\n534\tResults persist; the canvas has memory.\n535\t\n536\t- Session store (SQLite, 7 tables)\n537\t- Topic model: canvas shows one card per active topic, updated in place\n538\t- Telegram surface fallback (reuse telegram-claude-bridge)\n539\t- Bead watcher: closed NEEDLE beads push results to active surface\n540\t- Workload summary on reconnect\n541\t- Staleness indicators on cards\n542\t\n543\tDeliverable: sessions that survive browser refresh; Telegram fallback working.\n544\t\n545\t### Phase 2 — Self-Improvement Loop (~2 weeks)\n546\t\n547\tThe interface can be improved by talking into it.\n548\t\n549\t- Self-modification agent (Claude Code via NEEDLE)\n550\t- Hot-reload confirmed at every artifact layer\n551\t- Component library: UI-regen agent generates first components from actual result shapes\n552\t- Canvas live-updates when a component is versioned\n553\t- Explicit feedback processed: \"always include X\" → prompt updated → hot-reloaded\n554\t\n555\tDeliverable: at least one end-to-end self-modification cycle working (user instructs change, diff surfaced, approved, takes effect without redeploy).\n556\t\n557\t### Phase 3 — Responsiveness (~2-3 weeks)\n558\t\n559\tThe interface feels alive, not just reactive.\n560\t\n561\t- Ambient monitoring: active topics watched for state changes\n562\t- Diff-aware results: show what changed since last result\n563\t- Pre-warmed context: active topics refreshed in background every N minutes\n564\t- Multi-turn within topic: follow-up questions deepen current topic context\n565\t- Speculative pre-fetch: common follow-up patterns pre-fetched\n566\t- Notification batching in audio mode\n567\t- Implicit feedback signals fed to background analysis bead\n568\t\n569\tDeliverable: monitoring fires unprompted for a watched topic; follow-up questions are visibly faster.\n570\t\n571\t### Phase 4 — Audio Surface (~1-2 weeks)\n572\t\n573\tFull audio mode via Realtime API.\n574\t\n575\t- Realtime API voice session replaces text input path\n576\t- Tool-as-trigger model: `dispatch_intent()` returns ack, result arrives async\n577\t- Urgency-tiered voice narration\n578\t- Audio-to-canvas session continuity\n579\t\n580\tDeliverable: full voice session with canvas catch-up on surface switch.\n581\t\n582\t---\n583\t\n584\t## Self-Improvement: Hot-Reload Architecture\n585\t\n586\tEvery artifact that encodes behavior is readable, writable, and reloaded per-invocation:\n587\t\n588\t| Behavior | Artifact | Reload point |\n589\t|----------|----------|-------------|\n590\t| Utterance segmentation | `prompts/router.md` | Each router call |\n591\t| Intent→project routing | `config/registry.yaml` | Each router call |\n592\t| Context fetch strategy | `prompts/fetch/{type}.md` | Each fetch invocation |\n593\t| Result format and detail | `prompts/synthesize.md` | Each synthesize call |\n594\t| Voice narration style | `prompts/voice.md` | Each session turn |\n595\t| Urgency classification | `prompts/urgency.md` | Each escalate call |\n596\t| Visual rendering | Component library (DB) | Each card render |\n597\t| Monitoring rules | `config/monitoring.yaml` | Each monitoring tick |\n598\t\n599\tPer-invocation reload is the implementation strategy (read file, check mtime). File watching adds complexity for no benefit — prompts change rarely and file reads are cheap."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ac4673a6-a2b5-4d2d-8e25-0ea1a4bc7b08","uuid":"ae1188bc-f641-4f45-9a76-5cb0e480f850","timestamp":"2026-06-07T14:13:33.871Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/coding/aide-de-camp/docs/plan/plan.md","content":" The FastAPI server is the intelligence layer — it handles SSE connections, maintains session state, runs the router and synthesize strands, and serves the frontend HTML. There is no CDN path (no CF Pages).\n\n### Why not static\n\n- SSE connections are long-lived; CDNs cannot proxy them\n- WebSocket for the Realtime API voice session requires a persistent backend\n- The session store (SQLite) and artifact store (prompts, registry) require a writable filesystem\n- Hot-reload depends on the running server reading updated files from disk on each invocation\n\n### Phased hosting\n\n**Phase 0 (Hetzner server directly)**\n\nRun FastAPI as a process on the Hetzner server itself, not in k8s. Simplest possible path:\n- NEEDLE workers and the aide-de-camp server share the same filesystem\n- Self-modification agent writes directly to `prompts/` and `config/` — hot-reload works without any coordination\n- Expose via Tailscale (the server is already on the mesh); no ingress config needed\n- SQLite DBs are local files; no PVC required\n\nNo container, no CI, no ArgoCD. Just `uvicorn src.main:app` managed by a long-running tmux session or systemd unit.\n\n**Phase 1+ (containerized, ardenone-cluster)**\n\nOnce session persistence and multi-surface routing are needed, containerize and move to k8s:\n\n```\nDocker image: ronaldraygun/aide-de-camp\nDeployment: ardenone-cluster, namespace: aide-de-camp\nPVC: /data/ (SATA, ReadWriteOnce)\n  /data/session.db        ← session store\n  /data/components.db     ← component library\n  /data/prompts/          ← hot-reloadable prompt files\n  /data/config/           ← registry.yaml, monitoring.yaml, exceptions.yaml\n```\n\nThe artifact store (prompts, registry) moves from the repo's working directory to the PVC. The self-modification agent updates artifacts via the aide-de-camp API (`PATCH /artifacts/{name}`), which writes to the PVC path the server reads from.\n\n### Traefik configuration for SSE and WebSocket\n\nTraefik's default response buffering breaks SSE. The IngressRoute needs:\n\n```yaml\n# IngressRoute annotations\ntraefik.ingress.kubernetes.io/router.middlewares: aide-de-camp-strip-prefix@kubernetescrd\n\n# Middleware: disable buffering, extend timeouts\napiVersion: traefik.io/v1alpha1\nkind: Middleware\nmetadata:\n  name: aide-de-camp-streaming\nspec:\n  buffering:\n    maxResponseBodyBytes: 0   # disable buffering\n  headers:\n    customResponseHeaders:\n      X-Accel-Buffering: \"no\"\n```\n\nServersTransport timeout:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: traefik.io/v1alpha1\nkind: ServersTransport\nmetadata:\n  name: aide-de-camp-longlived\nspec:\n  forwardingTimeouts:\n    responseHeaderTimeout: 0    # no timeout on SSE streams\n    dialTimeout: 5s\n```\n\nDUCK-E's existing WebSocket IngressRoute config is the reference implementation for this cluster.\n\n### SQLite concurrency\n\nMultiple writers (bead watcher, background analysis bead, session handler) require WAL mode to avoid lock contention:\n\n```python\n# On DB open\nconn.execute(\"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL\")\nconn.execute(\"PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL\")\n```\n\nWAL mode allows concurrent reads during writes and serializes multiple writers without blocking. For a personal single-user app, this is sufficient through Phase 3. A server database (Postgres) is not needed.\n\n### adc CLI connectivity\n\nThe `adc` CLI is a thin HTTP client. It talks to the running server over Tailscale:\n\n```bash\n# ~/.config/adc/config\nserver_url = \"http://aide-de-camp.ardenone.com\"   # or localhost in Phase 0\n```\n\nNo local inference. The CLI sends requests to the FastAPI backend and streams the SSE response to the terminal. On the Hetzner server in Phase 0, `server_url = \"http://localhost:8000\"`.\n\n### CI/CD (Phase 1+)\n\nNew Argo WorkflowTemplate `aide-de-camp-build` on iad-ci:\n- Docker build → `ronaldraygun/aide-de-camp`\n- Update image tag in `jedarden/declarative-config` (k8s/ardenone-cluster/aide-de-camp/)\n- ArgoCD syncs automatically\n\nSame pattern as every other containerized service in the stack.\n\n---\n\n## Technology Stack\n\n| Layer | Choice | Reason |\n|-------|--------|--------|\n| Backend | FastAPI (Python) | Reuse DUCK-E scaffolding; SSE + WebSocket support; async-native |\n| STT | Web Speech API → whisper-stt fallback | Zero-latency browser-native; whisper-stt already deployed |\n| Voice session | OpenAI Realtime API (via DUCK-E session handler) | DUCK-E scaffolding already built on this |\n| LLM calls | ZAI proxy (`llm-proxy.ardenone.com`) | Pay-per-token, no subscription pressure on hot path |\n| Task workers | NEEDLE + Claude Code | Existing infrastructure, unchanged |\n| Session store | SQLite (WAL mode) | Lightweight, local, additive-only schema; single-user app |\n| Artifact store | PVC-mounted filesystem (Phase 1+) / local filesystem (Phase 0) | Writable at runtime; hot-reload reads per-invocation |\n| Frontend | Vanilla JS + Web Components | No build pipeline; SSE consumer + client-side card renderer |\n| Phase 0 hosting | Hetzner server, local process | Simplest path; shared filesystem with NEEDLE workers |\n| Phase 1+ hosting | ardenone-cluster, k8s Deployment | Behind existing Traefik + Tailscale ingress |\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Phases\n\n### Phase 0 — Minimal Viable Surface (~2 days)\n\nValidates the core question: does routing + parallel dispatch reduce friction?\n\n- Single HTML page: textarea + mic button (Web Speech API)\n- `POST /dispatch` endpoint: router → N parallel synthesize calls → SSE stream\n- Results appear as basic cards as agents resolve\n- No persistence, no auth, no component library, no ambient push\n\nDeliverable: the core query loop working end-to-end.\n\n### Phase 1 — Session and Topics (~1 week)\n\nResults persist; the canvas has memory.\n\n- Session store (SQLite, 7 tables)\n- Topic model: canvas shows one card per active topic, updated in place\n- Telegram surface fallback (reuse telegram-claude-bridge)\n- Bead watcher: closed NEEDLE beads push results to active surface\n- Workload summary on reconnect\n- Staleness indicators on cards\n\nDeliverable: sessions that survive browser refresh; Telegram fallback working.\n\n### Phase 2 — Self-Improvement Loop (~2 weeks)\n\nThe interface can be improved by talking into it.\n\n- Self-modification agent (Claude Code via NEEDLE)\n- Hot-reload confirmed at every artifact layer\n- Component library: UI-regen agent generates first components from actual result shapes\n- Canvas live-updates when a component is versioned\n- Explicit feedback processed: \"always include X\" → prompt updated → hot-reloaded\n\nDeliverable: at least one end-to-end self-modification cycle working (user instructs change, diff surfaced, approved, takes effect without redeploy).\n\n### Phase 3 — Responsiveness (~2-3 weeks)\n\nThe interface feels alive, not just reactive.\n\n- Ambient monitoring: active topics watched for state changes\n- Diff-aware results: show what changed since last result\n- Pre-warmed context: active topics refreshed in background every N minutes\n- Multi-turn within topic: follow-up questions deepen current topic context\n- Speculative pre-fetch: common follow-up patterns pre-fetched\n- Notification batching in audio mode\n- Implicit feedback signals fed to background analysis bead\n\nDeliverable: monitoring fires unprompted for a watched topic; follow-up questions are visibly faster.\n\n### Phase 4 — Audio Surface (~1-2 weeks)\n\nFull audio mode via Realtime API.\n\n- Realtime API voice session replaces text input path\n- Tool-as-trigger model: `dispatch_intent()` returns ack, result arrives async\n- Urgency-tiered voice narration\n- Audio-to-canvas session continuity\n\nDeliverable: full voice session with canvas catch-up on surface switch.\n\n---\n\n## Self-Improvement: Hot-Reload Architecture\n\nEvery artifact that encodes behavior is readable, writable, and reloaded per-invocation:\n\n| Behavior | Artifact | Reload point |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| Utterance segmentation | `prompts/router.md` | Each router call |\n| Intent→project routing | `config/registry.yaml` | Each router call |\n| Context fetch strategy | `prompts/fetch/{type}.md` | Each fetch invocation |\n| Result format and detail | `prompts/synthesize.md` | Each synthesize call |\n| Voice narration style | `prompts/voice.md` | Each session turn |\n| Urgency classification | `prompts/urgency.md` | Each escalate call |\n| Visual rendering | Component library (DB) | Each card render |\n| Monitoring rules | `config/monitoring.yaml` | Each monitoring tick |\n\nPer-invocation reload is the implementation strategy (read file, check mtime). File watching adds complexity for no benefit — prompts change rarely and file reads are cheap.","numLines":300,"startLine":300,"totalLines":659}}}

communications, handles any category of task — research, logistics, coordination, personal matters — and is specifically attached to *one* commanding officer, not a generic service.\n\nThis captures what the system is: not a coding assistant, not a voice interface, not a routing layer — a universal personal interface that handles anything the user asks, knows their full operational context, and improves through use.\n\n## CLI Invocation\n\nThe CLI uses `adc` — the standard abbreviation for aide-de-camp.\n\n```bash\nadc dispatch \"has the options pipeline caught up? also check the ibkr mcp
